Uncrowned pieces can move only diagonally forward; kings can move in any diagonal direction.\r\nA jump consists of moving a piece from a square diagonally adjacent to an opponent's piece, to an empty square immediately beyond it in the same direction. (Thus jumping over the opponent's piece.) Uncrowned pieces can jump only diagonally forward; kings can jump in any diagonal direction.
